I feel like most people don't do the Iron Golem method, because:  A.) It's a lot harder to gather so much iron in a single player survival. Let alone on harder difficulties. B.) Iron golems, and by extension Withers, are pretty unpredictable. They'll agro and de-agro for seemingly no reason, and can be badly affected by lag or slow devices. C.) On some worlds it's very hard to find pumpkins. Not to mention some of the older, casual players don't even know how to obtain Carved Pumpkins. Since they used to just be the default pumpkin block. D.) The Wither is a scary, and unnecessary boss for most players. The only reason you'd need it is an Ender Chest or Beacon, neither of which are particularly useful if you're not an expert builder. F.) It's definitely a pride thing. It's incredibly impressive to beat something considered world destroying in lore. Not to mention the Wither is very hard to create and has a good arsenal of options to destroy you and the world forever. By extension, the achievement you get for defeating the Wither is a pride thing as well.  Just my opinion and rationale as to why people don't use Iron Golems for the Wither. It's honestly a pretty smart ploy for a large server of expert players. You'll need a lot of Nether Stars for Ender Chests and Beacons. Definitely feel free to include more reasons below.

To anyone! The best place to mine is -58 and when you find diamonds mine on a direct straight line from the diamonds on coordinate. (Ex: positive x) if you don't find any diamonds in the next hundred blocks then you need to go FROM THE DIAMONDS on the (Ex: z coordinate) and you should find some. (it doesn't matter if it's Positive or Negative). I did this and in about 15 - 30 mins I got about 2 stacks. I would recommend a few stacks of torches, eff 3, 4, 5, unbreaking, 1, 2, 3 and a fortune 3 pick. Caves work but in the new update if diamonds spawn next to "Cave Air" they are most likely to be 1-3 veins, while in strip mining it tends to be 4-8 veins.\

grian, because you are experimenting with colour and copper more this season, you might need a tip. You can cheapen how many blocks you get by crafting regular copper. Let me explain. Normally, you would craft 4 copper blocks into 4 cut copper, but if you use a stonecutter, then one copper block will make 4 cut copper. Just to help cut down on the cost
There is a fun trick involving chests and item frames. You can place item frames on the sides where the chests are almost touching. It will look like they are stuck together by a piece of wood.

I would love to see a modded hermitcraft series, stuff like villager trading gets removed, mining veins are lowered or outright removed. Instead there is a giant mall at spawn that sells everything you could possibly want but only takes a specific currency. This currency is earned by either trading in bulk mining results (think an inventory full of cobble for a stack of iron ore)  or by rare veins in the world but mostly from mini-dungeons you can find in the world, some designed for 1 hermit, others for multiples (honestly this stuff could be added as needed too). 5:55 â€œGeneral Scar, you are a Bold one.â€
The reason no one use iron golems for wither fights, is that there are way more efficient ways to kill the wither. The beast way is using contraptions. But for early game the best way is to dig a long corridor 1x2 then after like 30 block make a 3x3x3 (digging up one block) room. Then spawn the wither. Then all you have to do is keep swinging at the wither wile backing up. A Wither is 3 block tall and shoots from its head meaning that it can see you and will chase you but are unable to attack you.  The bonus of this tactic is that when the Wither is dead. It will have cleard out a 3-5 block tunnel revealing ores= u might get diamonds from doing it.

I'm curious about what the new villager set up will look like. In my current Minecraft world I made a villager trading hall with 32 villagers in a square. Each villager has a bed, and an opening so they can talk to their neighbors and summon an iron golem. The iron golems spawn on a large square platform with water pushing them to a central kill chamber. Around all this there is a moat with water pushing to a separate kill chamber for other mobs. That one doubles as a raid farm. None of them are particularly efficient, but it is nice having an all in one set up that didn't need any redstone. I haven't used any mined diamonds to get fully equipped with tools and armor.

idea for hc9 lore: Grian, you are one of few sole survivors of the hc8 disaster. When the moon collided with hc8 you escaped through a rocket with your fellow Hermits. When you landed you found yourself along a rocky coast with one rock in particular sticking out. you walked over to examine it. Later That day you set up base next to the specimen wich you decided to call The Entity. When you woke up it had grown to a size bigger than you could ever imagine. A tip with copper: If oxidized copper is connected to less oxidized copper, the less oxidized copper will oxidize MUCH faster. Better to make a giant copper block than to spread out all the copper. (Or a giant square if you want to remove copper at certain states.) One part gets oxidized and the rest matches the oxidation state very quickly.

I know no one asked, but I have a story for the Entity: It was just a rock, when villagers started reporting strange things popping out of the side of it. The sightings ranged from trees, to copper, to honey, with seemingly no rhyme of reason. That is, until someone found the crack. A small break in the side of the boulder soon grew to a full entrance. Inside were stocks of all the things popping up on the outside, and as the news spread, people started getting curious. And greedy. The supplies in there were worth a fortune! But of course, the Entity knew this as well. As one unfortunate soul learned, the Entity had a defense mechanism. Anyone who tried to take the goods without leaving a diamond or two payment would be swallowed by the Entity, never to be seen again. He is not Grian he is Pian
Iron golems are how I farm withers too lol. Their are 2 flaws to this method but are easy to overcome. 1) the wither tends to fly above mobs attacking it, including players. Building a tunnel like this and baiting it to the golems will work for a bit, but eventually it will blow out enough ceiling that the golems cant reach. Solve this by spawning the wither in the end, under the end portal. The bedrock trap still works in 1.18 and will keep the wither at the same height. Then the 2nd problem will be easier to manage as well.  2) at a certain point iron golems will stop attacking the wither. I dont know why but they will just stand there and get blown up. They de-aggro then wont aggro again on that particular wither. This is solved by using a minimum of 3 golems. The combined damage will be enough to kill the wither before they de aggro and they will aggro the next wither as usual.

I had an idea for the truth behind the Entity, it's basically a living rock, so biologically, that's pretty odd in Earth standards. So I have brainstormed about the biochemistry of the boulder, and I wanted to share it, c'mon, Grian could even see this somehow, and I wanted to know what y'all think. So the Entity could be a silicon-based lifeform, which means it can't exist like a normal motile animal in oxygen rich environments, so the best there is for Earth like environments would be a lifeform that looks like a boulder, now why is that? When silicon is found with oxygen, it reacts to create various silicon oxides, which are rocky crystals, so the boulder could use the oxygen from the atmosphere to create an outer rocky shell composed of several silicates and quartzes, both are present in most rocks on Earth so a normal looking boulder is just right, it could also use oxygen to protect their internal organs, like it's heart, which is a conduit, that kinda has something of an outer shell. As for ways of obtaining energy, it could use chemotrophy, chemotrophy is the process of oxidizing several metals to obtain energy, this kind of bioenergetic process is most found in deep sea trenches around hydrothermal vents, but the boulder is in the surface, so what could happen is that the entity stretches specialized roots all over the land to sustain it's needs for metals, eventually stretching over to volcanically active places to get more energy, another solution would be to use phototrophy of some sorts, having specialized pigments beneath thin rocky layers from their shell to absorb the sun's energy somehow, and perhaps even having a kind of mutualistic relationships with the plants that grow on it, the plants provide carbon and nitrogen so it can breathe better as plants are more well adapted to it, as well as extra sunlight, and the entity could provide free nutrients from their shell and no competition with other plants. So that's what I have until now, what do y'all think about it, it probably has some things that could be better but rn this is the best I have! So anyway that was a great video and all- and I'm also imagining all the kinds of different themes the village could take! This Gon be awesome, season 9 is certainly starting with the right foot

Hey Grian, I don't know if you already know this or not, but you can actually apply wax to the copper in your inventory without needing to place it. Also, if you wax the copper blocks before turning them into cut copper blocks or stairs the resulting cut copper will also already be waxed, which should end up saving you wax. Might make building with copper slightly less annoying in the future.

Day 1: when I first came upon the entity, I thought it nothing but a mossy rock, unusual geology for the surrounding grasslands but not far fetched, then I heard it, a heart beat coming from within the mossy stone, i was enamoured, I have now begun this journal to keep track of the discoveries I find as I continue my study of this entity  Day 3: with 2 days of sample taking I uncovered a hole inside only to discover the entity is hollow, I cannot find the source of the heartbeat but it is forever present  Day 7: as I build my future lab and temporary home I stored some wooden logs near the entity and left to go hunting for food, when I returned the logs were halfway absorbed by the entity, now the logs have been fully absorbed and a medium sized tree sapling has grown into a light wooded willow tree on top of the entity, fascinating as it is, this requires further study, even now the hollow interior has changed, a corner of the cave is made of wood bark and is slowly expanding outwards into a shape I cannot discern just yet  Day 8: the bark has now become a fully functional chest of wood, when I open it I found a spacious box filled with logs. When I close and reopen there are more logs, I believe this entity can absorb and continuously reproduce material by dragging matter from underneath and nearby to fill these chests with material, this requires further study. Next I will leave ingots and blocks of copper to see if the entity will absorb and produce like with the logs to prove my theory correct.
